Cejtlin's Old Church Slavonic Dictionary

To search in this dictionary, use ctrl+F (or your browser's equivalent command for searching for text within the current page) and type the OCS word that you want to query (without apostrophes or diacritics). When you find the term you're looking for, click on the link to open an image, which will display the dictionary entry. You will probably find it helpful to have a way of typing Old Cyrillic characters! (But you could live without those that have an asterisk.)


If you find any errors, please write to me at j.walker@cantab.net
